[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAn AddressSanitizer report indicates a heap-based buffer overflow in libxml2’s HTML[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparser. Specifically, during fuzz testing of the `html` utility, a multi-byte write[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moverruns a heap allocation in the `htmlSecureComment` function, leading to an [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mout-of-bounds write immediately past the allocated buffer.[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue Manifestation  [0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  The crash occurs when running the `html` binary under libFuzzer with [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAddressSanitizer enabled. The fuzzer invokes `LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput`, which calls [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minto `htmlCtxtParseDocument`. During parsing of an HTML comment, control flows into[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`htmlSecureComment` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mvia `htmlTopParseComment`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, where a call to `memcpy` writes [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m105[0m[39m bytes just past the end of a [0m[1;36m501[0m[39m-byte heap allocation, triggering ASan’s [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mheap-buffer-overflow detection.[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Vulnerability Type  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  This is a heap-based buffer overflow: data copied via `memcpy` exceeds the size [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mof the target allocation.[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Key Observations  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The corrupted address [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m0x515000000775[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is exactly [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m bytes past a [0m[1;36m501[0m[39m-byte heap [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mblock allocated by `xmlFuzzMalloc`.  [0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The overflow happens in `HTMLparser.c` at line [0m[1;36m3591[0m[39m inside `htmlSecureComment`.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The offending write originates from an unbounded or miscomputed length passed [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto `memcpy`.  [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The fuzzer harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`fuzz/html.c`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m simply drives the parser and is not the root[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcause; it exposes the flaw in `HTMLparser.c`.[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Areas for Further Investigation  [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. The implementation of `htmlSecureComment` in `HTMLparser.c`, especially buffer[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msize computations and the arguments to `memcpy`.  [0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. The allocation logic in `xmlFuzzMalloc` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfuzz.c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to confirm requested size [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mversus actual buffer size.  [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. The surrounding comment parsing logic in `htmlTopParseComment` and [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`htmlParseDocument` to understand input bounds and state management.  [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Any auxiliary functions or data structures involved in storing or sanitizing [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcomment text within the HTML parser.[0m                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparserInternals.[0m[1;92mc:2800[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m2806[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2800[0m[39m:    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mctxt->spaceTab == NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2801[0m[39m:   [0m[39mctxt->spaceTab = [0m[1;35mxmlMalloc[0m[1;39m([0m[39minitialNodeTabSize * [0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mint[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2802[0m[39m:   [0m[39mctxt->spaceMax = initialNodeTabSize;[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2803[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2804[0m[39m:    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mctxt->spaceTab == NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2805[0m[39m:   [0m[1;35mreturn[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m-1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2806[0m[39m:    ctxt->spaceNr = [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m;[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparser.[0m[1;92mc:5330[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m5337[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5330[0m[39m:   [0m[39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnbchar > [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5331[0m[39m:            if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf == NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5332[0m[39m:                if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39m*in == [0m[32m'-'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m && [0m[1;39m([0m[39min[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m][0m[39m == [0m[32m'-'[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5333[0m[39m:                    size = nbchar + [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m;[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5334[0m[39m:                else[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5335[0m[39m:                    size = XML_PARSER_BUFFER_SIZE + nbchar;[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5336[0m[39m:                buf = [0m[1;35mxmlMalloc[0m[1;39m([0m[39msize[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5337[0m[39m:                if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf == NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparser.[0m[1;92mc:5341[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m5349[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5341[0m[39m:                len = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5342[0m[39m:            [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m else if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlen + nbchar + [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m >= size[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5343[0m[39m:                xmlChar *new_buf;[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5344[0m[39m:                size  += len + nbchar + XML_PARSER_BUFFER_SIZE;[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5345[0m[39m:                new_buf = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mxmlChar *[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;35mxmlRealloc[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf, size[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5346[0m[39m:                if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnew_buf == NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5347[0m[39m:                    xmlFree [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5348[0m[39m:                    [0m[1;35mxmlErrMemory[0m[1;39m([0m[39mctxt[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5349[0m[39m:                    return;[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause Analysis  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The function `htmlSecureComment` in HTMLparser.c misuses `ctxt->spaceTab` [0m[1;39m([0m[39man [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`int*` classification table[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m as a byte buffer for accumulating comment text.  [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - It initializes `buffer_size = ctxt->spaceMax` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnumber of ints[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and `buffer = [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mxmlChar*[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mctxt->spaceTab`, then, when `spaceTab` is NULL, falls back to a small [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdefault [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m500[0m[39m bytes[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. In both cases it treats that storage as a byte-array of length[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`buffer_size`, causing out-of-bounds writes when comment sizes exceed that value.[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Preserve Existing Logic  [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All higher-level parsing and sanitization logic [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthe loops that examine each [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcharacter or chunk of the comment and apply sanitization rules[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m must remain [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munchanged.  [0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The only change is in how the accumulation buffer is allocated and resized. [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe contract of `htmlSecureComment`—taking an input comment buffer and length, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msanitizing it, freeing the old one, and returning a newly allocated, [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnull-terminated buffer—stays the same.  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Patch Implementation Steps  [0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Remove any use of `ctxt->spaceTab` and `ctxt->spaceMax` within [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`htmlSecureComment`. They are not intended for comment storage.  [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Introduce a dedicated `xmlChar *buffer` and an integer `buffer_size` computed[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfrom the actual input length [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`len`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m plus a safety margin [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`XML_PARSER_BUFFER_SIZE`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m or simply `len + [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m`.  [0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. On entry to `htmlSecureComment` [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround lines [0m[1;36m3330[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m3336[0m[39m in HTMLparser.c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:  [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Drop the assignments  [0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          used = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;  [0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          buffer_size = ctxt->spaceMax;  [0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          buffer = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mxmlChar *[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mctxt->spaceTab;  [0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Instead compute:  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          buffer_size = len + [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m;  [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          buffer = [0m[1;35mxmlMalloc[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuffer_size[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;  [0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuffer == NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[1;35mxmlFree[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcomment[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;  [0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[1;35mxmlErrMemory[0m[1;39m([0m[39mctxt[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[1;35mreturn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mNULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m  [0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          used = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;  [0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   d. Retain the same per-chunk sanitization loop that computes `chunkSize` and [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcopies bytes via `memcpy`, but update the resize logic:  [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Before each `memcpy`, check  [0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mused + chunkSize + [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m > buffer_size[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m  [0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              int new_size = [0m[1;35mMAX[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuffer_size * [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m, used + chunkSize + [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;  [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              xmlChar *tmp = [0m[1;35mxmlRealloc[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuffer, new_size[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;  [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp == NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m  [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                [0m[1;35mxmlFree[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuffer[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;  [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                [0m[1;35mxmlFree[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcomment[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;  [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                [0m[1;35mxmlErrMemory[0m[1;39m([0m[39mctxt[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;  [0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                [0m[1;35mreturn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mNULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;  [0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m  [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              buffer = tmp;  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              buffer_size = new_size;  [0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   e. At loop exit, terminate:  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          buffer[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mused[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;35mxmlFree[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcomment[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;35mreturn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuffer[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   f. Remove references to `spaceTab`[0m[35m/[0m[39m`spaceMax` in this function; they should [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mremain live for their original use elsewhere but will not be co-opted.[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Justification  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This guarantees the accumulation buffer is sized strictly in bytes, based on [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe actual input length, eliminating any mismatch between element-count and [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbyte-count assumptions.  [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - It follows the proven pattern used in `xmlParseComment` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mparser.[0m[1;92mc:5330[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m5349[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhich always allocates a dedicated `xmlChar*` buffer and grows it safely.  [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No changes are made to the fuzz harness, test code, or external libraries. The[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpatch strictly confines itself to HTMLparser.c and preserves all existing [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msanitization logic.  [0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Potential Side Effects & Mitigation  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Memory usage for very large comments may increase [0m[1;39m([0m[39msince we allocate `len+[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m` [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mup front[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. However, this mirrors the original input size, and comments rarely [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mapproach parser memory limits.  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Doubling the buffer on growth ensures amortized linear performance, matching [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mother parts of the parser.  [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All existing callers of `htmlSecureComment` continue to get a freshly [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallocated, null-terminated buffer, so there is no change to function signatures or [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mownership semantics.  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Ensure that any error path frees both the old comment buffer and the partially[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallocated new buffer, then reports memory errors via `[0m[1;35mxmlErrMemory[0m[1;39m([0m[39mctxt[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.  [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAn AddressSanitizer report surfaced a heap-buffer-overflow in libxml2’s HTML parser[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhen fuzzing the `htmlSecureComment` routine. The overflow occurs during a `memcpy`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mof a comment chunk into a buffer that is too small. A patch was attempted to grow [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe buffer dynamically before copying, but the patch failed to compile. The errors [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpoint to an undeclared identifier `comment` and an implicit call to `xmlErrMemory`,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mindicating missing declarations or scope issues in the patch context.[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Initial Issue  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The fuzzer exercised `LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput`, which invokes [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`htmlCtxtParseDocument`.  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Inside `htmlSecureComment`, a chunk of data is copied into a `buffer` [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallocated earlier via `xmlFuzzMalloc`.  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - AddressSanitizer reports that `[0m[1;35mmemcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuffer + used, chunk, chunkSize[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` writes[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbeyond the [0m[1;36m501[0m[39m-byte region, triggering a heap-buffer-overflow.[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Important Observations  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The overflow write is of size [0m[1;36m105[0m[39m bytes immediately after the allocated [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mregion.  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The stack trace pins the overflow to `__asan_memcpy` called from line [0m[1;36m3591[0m[39m in [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`HTMLparser.c`.  [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The offending buffer is initially sized to the length of the comment plus one [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand never grown thereafter.  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The heap allocation originates from `xmlFuzzMalloc`, confirming that the [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuffer comes from the parser’s internal fuzz-malloc wrapper.[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Patch Attempt  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - A guard was added before `memcpy` to check whether `used + chunkSize + [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m` [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwould exceed `buffer_size`.  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - If the check fails, the code doubles `buffer_size` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mor adjusts it to exactly [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfit[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and calls `xmlRealloc`.  [0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - On reallocation failure, the code attempts cleanup by freeing `buffer` and [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcalling `[0m[1;35mxmlFree[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mxmlChar *[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mcomment[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and then `[0m[1;35mxmlErrMemory[0m[1;39m([0m[39mctxt[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.  [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - After successful growth, `[0m[1;35mmemcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39m&buffer[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mused[0m[1;39m][0m[39m, chunk, chunkSize[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` is retried.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Patch Result  [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Compilation failed with an error: `use of undeclared identifier [0m[32m'comment'[0m[39m`. [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis identifier is not in scope at the patch site.  [0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - A warning flagged `xmlErrMemory` as an implicit function, meaning its [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprototype was not visible in that translation unit.  [0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - An unused-parameter warning appeared for `maxLength`, indicating that [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msurrounding code signatures may not align with the patch.  [0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - As a result, the library’s build process aborted with errors, and the fuzzers [0m [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3579[0m[39m:            xmlChar *tmp = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mxmlChar *[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;35mxmlRealloc[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuffer, newSize + [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3580[0m[39m:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3581[0m[39m:            if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp == NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3582[0m[39m:                [0m[1;35mhtmlErrMemory[0m[1;39m([0m[39mctxt[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3583[0m[39m:                goto error;[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3584[0m[39m:            [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3585[0m[39m:            buffer = tmp;[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3586[0m[39m:            buffer_size = newSize;[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mHTMLparser.[0m[1;92mc:3618[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m3627[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3618[0m[39m:    ret = [0m[1;35mxmlMalloc[0m[1;39m([0m[39mused + [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3619[0m[39m:    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mret == NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3620[0m[39m:        [0m[1;35mhtmlErrMemory[0m[1;39m([0m[39mctxt[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3621[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m else [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3622[0m[39m:        [0m[1;35mmemcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mret, buffer, used[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3623[0m[39m:        ret[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mused[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3624[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3625[0m[39m:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;92m3626:e[0m[39mrror:[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3627[0m[39m:    ctxt->spaceTab = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mvoid *[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m buffer;[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparser.[0m[1;92mc:223[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m226[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m223[0m[39m:static void[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m224[0m[39m:[0m[1;35mxmlErrMemory[0m[1;39m([0m[39mxmlParserCtxtPtr ctxt[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m225[0m[39m:    [0m[1;35mxmlCtxtErrMemory[0m[1;39m([0m[39mctxt[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m226[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Summary of Root Cause  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   The heap-buffer-overflow in htmlSecureComment stems from an incorrect [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreallocation check. The existing code only grows the buffer when `extraSize > [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuffer_size`, ignoring the already‐used bytes. Consequently, when `used + extraSize[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m+ [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m` exceeds `buffer_size` but `extraSize` alone does not, the code skips the [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreallocation and overruns the buffer. The previous patch attempted to graft a new [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mguard clause further down, but it:[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Used an out-of-scope identifier `comment`.[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Called the wrong error handler [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`xmlErrMemory` instead of `htmlErrMemory`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Introduced duplicated logic and compilation errors.[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Patch Scope  [0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   We must modify only the reallocation logic in `htmlSecureComment` within [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mHTMLparser.c. We will:[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Remove the failed patch block [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines ~[0m[1;36m3588[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m3596[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Adjust the existing “grow‐if‐too‐small” clause at lines [0m[1;36m3577[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m3586[0m[39m to correctly[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39maccount for `used + extraSize + [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m`.[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Keep the standard error path [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[1;35mhtmlErrMemory[0m[1;39m([0m[39mctxt[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` → `goto error`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and leave [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mall harness, utility, and test code untouched.[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Detailed Steps  [0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Locate in HTMLparser.c the buffer‐growth block [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround line [0m[1;36m3577[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mextraSize > buffer_size[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          size_t newSize = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mused + extraSize[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m * [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m;[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          xmlChar *tmp = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mxmlChar *[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;35mxmlRealloc[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuffer, newSize + [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp == NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              [0m[1;35mhtmlErrMemory[0m[1;39m([0m[39mctxt[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              goto error;[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          buffer = tmp;[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          buffer_size = newSize;[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Change the `if` condition to ensure there is room for the existing data plus [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe incoming chunk plus a NUL terminator:[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mused + extraSize + [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m > buffer_size[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Revise the growth calculation to double the old size but also guarantee it’s [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mat least `used + extraSize + [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m`:[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          size_t newSize = buffer_size * [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m;[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnewSize < used + extraSize + [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              newSize = used + extraSize + [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m;[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          xmlChar *tmp = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mxmlChar *[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;35mxmlRealloc[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuffer, newSize + [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   d. Leave the error‐handling path unchanged, calling `[0m[1;35mhtmlErrMemory[0m[1;39m([0m[39mctxt[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`goto error`.  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   e. Ensure after reallocation you assign:[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          buffer = tmp;[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          buffer_size = newSize;[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   f. Remove the previously added patch at lines ~[0m[1;36m3588[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m3596[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthe extra guard/memcpy[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mblock that referenced `comment` and `xmlErrMemory`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Preservation of Logic  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We keep the existing progressive‐parsing loop, the use of [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`ctxt->spaceTab/spaceMax` as the buffer bootstrap, and the final copy into `ret`.  [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We continue to report memory failures via `[0m[1;35mhtmlErrMemory[0m[1;39m([0m[39mctxt[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and unwind via[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe `error` label, which stores the [0m[1;39m([0m[39mpossibly reallocated[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m buffer back into [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`ctxt->spaceTab` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mand, in the original code, also updates `ctxt->spaceMax` further [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdown[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Addressing Compilation Errors  [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No undeclared symbols [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`comment` is never used[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We rely solely on `htmlErrMemory`, whose prototype is already visible to [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mHTMLparser.c.  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We do not introduce any new headers or external dependencies.[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Potential Side Effects & Mitigations  [0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The new reallocation condition prevents any overflow, even when parsing [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mextremely large comments, by growing the buffer appropriately.  [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Doubling the buffer size amortizes the cost of repeated reallocations.  [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - In worst‐case modes [0m[1;39m([0m[39mprogressive parsing[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, this may increase memory usage, but[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39monly as needed to fit the data.  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The error path remains identical, so any existing tests for out‐of‐memory [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconditions will still pass.[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. References & Similar Patterns  [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This approach mirrors how the XML parser’s `xmlParseCDataBlock` grows its [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuffer, checking against `used + length + [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m`.  [0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - It follows the same `xmlRealloc` → `error` label pattern already present in [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mHTMLparser.c.[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mBy making only this localized change to the overflow check, we fully prevent the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mheap‐buffer‐overflow, restore successful compilation, and preserve all existing [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunctionality and error‐reporting behavior. [0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
